Fomat_TMA 02_Med_Radio_TMED 
VAR result =
    AVERAGE ( Fact_EasyMedia4_30m[Total Segundos TMED#] )
VAR hh =
    IF (
        LEN (
            ROUNDDOWN (
                result / 3600,
                0
            )
        ) = 1,
        "0"
            & ROUNDDOWN (
                result / 3600,
                0
            ),
        ROUNDDOWN (
            result / 3600,
            0
        )
    )
VAR mm =
    IF (
        LEN (
            ROUNDDOWN (
                ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
                0
            )
        ) = 1,
        "0"
            & ROUNDDOWN (
                ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
                0
            ),
        ROUNDDOWN (
            ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
            0
        )
    )
VAR ss =
    IF (
        LEN (
            MOD (
                result - ( hh * 3600 ),
                60
            )
        ) = 1,
        "0"
            & MOD (
                result - ( hh * 3600 ),
                60
            ),
        MOD (
            result - ( hh * 3600 ),
            60
        )
    )
RETURN
    IF (
        hh & ":" & mm & ":"
            & ROUND (
                ss,
                0
            ) = "::",
        BLANK (),
        hh & ":" & mm & ":"
            & IF (
                LEN (
                    ROUNDUP (
                        ss,
                        0
                    )
                ) = 1,
                "0"
                    & ROUNDDOWN (
                        ss,
                        0
                    ),
                ROUNDDOWN (
                    ss,
                    0
                )
            )
    )
  • Measure: Fomat_TMA
    • Table: Fact_EasyMedia4_30m
    • Column: Total Segundos TMED# (Table: Fact_EasyMedia4_30m)
 Measure: Fomat_TMA

    • Column: Praça (Table: DIM_Praça)

    IF (
        LEN (
            ROUNDDOWN (
                ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
                0
            )
        ) = 1,
        "0"
            & ROUNDDOWN (
                ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
                0
            ),
        ROUNDDOWN (
            ( result - ( hh * 3600 ) ) / 60,
            0
        )
    )
VAR ss =
    IF (
        LEN (
            MOD (
                result - ( hh * 3600 ),
                60
            )
        ) = 1,
        "0"
            & MOD (
                result - ( hh * 3600 ),
                60
            ),
        MOD (
            result - ( hh * 3600 ),
            60
        )
    )
RETURN
    IF (
        hh & ":" & mm & ":"
            & ROUND (
                ss,
                0
            ) = "::",
        BLANK (),
        hh & ":" & mm & ":"
            & IF (
                LEN (
                    ROUNDUP (
                        ss,
                        0
                    )
                ) = 1,
                "0"
                    & ROUNDDOWN (
                        ss,
                        0
                    ),
                ROUNDDOWN (
                    ss,
                    0
                )
            )
    )
  • Measure: Fomat_TMA_Turno
    • Table: Fact_EasyMedia4_Turno
    • Column: Total Segundos (Table: Fact_EasyMedia4_Turno)
  • Measure: Fomat_TMA_Turno
    • Measure: M.T.Cond.TMED

M.Shr.Bloco 08_Med_Radio_SHARE# 
VAR inicio =
    MIN ( 'DIM_Day Part'[Hora.1] )
VAR fim =
    MAX ( 'DIM_Day Part'[Hora.2] )
VAR bloco = inicio & " - " & fim
VAR turno =
    CALCULATE (
        ISFILTERED ( 'DIM_Day Part'[Turno] ),
        ALLSELECTED ( 'DIM_Day Part'[Turno] )
    )
VAR daypart = bloco
VAR texto =
    SELECTEDVALUE ( 'DIM_Day Part'[Turno] )
RETURN
    IF (
        turno,
        texto,
        "Bl 30min"
    )
//return bloco
